ef_on_monthly_pulse_recurence = {
	update_modifiers_bc_fc_ns = yes

	if  = {
		limit = {
			is_subject_custom_trigger = no
		}
		remove_suject_currency = yes
	}

	#for new country by revolution
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_revolutionary = yes
			not  = {
				has_variable = coal_release_quantity
			}
		}
		add_journal_entry = {
			type = for_new_country_je_2
		}
	}
}

# ef_on_monthly_pulse_reset = {
# }

central_bank_ef_on_monthly_pulse_country = {
	#central_bank_interest_actual = yes  #à quiu cela  sert ?
	#central_bank_gold_reserves_state = yes #à modifier pour unee valeur scripté

	fluctuations_money_value_1_month = yes
	government_loan_month = yes

	#inflation_value & modifier
	inflation_modifier = yes
	inflation_on_consumer_goods_market_value_fluctuations = yes
	inflation_on_energy_market_value_fluctuations = yes
	inflation_on_raw_material_market_value_fluctuations = yes
	inflation_on_manufactured_goods_market_value_fluctuations = yes
	inflation_on_military_equipment_market_value_fluctuations = yes
	money_value_dif_01_market_value_fluctuations = yes

	#monetary_policy_player
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_player = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				or = {
					not = {
						has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_policy
					}
					var:devaluation_on = 1
					var:revaluation_on = 1
				}
			}
			monetary_policy_inflation = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_law = law_type:law_no_monetary_policy
				or = {
					var:monetary_policy_inflation > 0
					var:monetary_policy_inflation < 0
				}
			}
			monetary_policy_inflation_reset = yes
		}
	}

	#stockpiling_currency_and_gold
	if  = {
		limit = {
			market.owner = root
			not  = {
				is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		stockpiling_currency_and_gold = yes
	}

	if  = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = foreign_exchange_controls
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				var:devaluation_on = 1
			}
			devaluation_on = yes
		}
		if  = {
			limit = {
				var:revaluation_on = 1
			}
			revaluation_on = yes
		}
	}
}

financial_center_ef_on_monthly_pulse_country = {

	if  = {
		limit  = {
			is_player = yes
			current_order > 0
		}
		RMSA_MMSA_order_trigger = yes
	}
}

national_stockpile_ef_on_monthly_pulse_country = {
	flow_storing_on_action = yes

	if  = {
		limit  = {
			has_modifier = has_national_stockpile
		}
		storing_releasing_on_action = yes
	}
}

ef_on_half_yearly_pulse_recurence = {
	currency_strength_modifier = yes

	#########################################
	#ai strategy
	#########################################
	ai_building_strategy = yes
	fluctuations_gdp_1_year = yes

	if = {
		limit = {
			market.owner = root
		}
		trade_balance = yes
	}
}

	}
}

financial_center_ef_on_half_yearly_pulse_country = {

	if  = {
		limit  = {
			country_indice > 5000000
		}
		fluctuations_country_indice_value_year = yes
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			country_indice < 5000000
			NOT = {
				stock_market_index = 100
			}
		}
		fluctuations_country_indice_value_year_clear = yes
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment > 0
		}
		interest_per_month_from_foreign_debt_investment = yes
	}
}

central_bank_ef_on_yearly_pulse_country = {

	cumulative_inflation_5_year = yes
	cumulative_inflation_10_year = yes
	cumulative_inflation_since_beginning = yes

	fluctuations_money_value_5_year = yes
	fluctuations_money_value_10_year = yes

	if = {
		limit = {
			is_ai = yes
			has_technology_researched = gold_standard
			not = {
				has_law = law_type:law_isolationism
				#is_subject_custom_trigger = yes #?
			}
		}
		ai_buy_sell_currency = yes
	}

	#credit_at_central
	if = {
		limit = {
			credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_month > 5
		}
		credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_week = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_modifier = interest_at_the_central_bank
			credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_month < 5
		}
		credit_at_central_bank_interest_per_week_off = yes
	}

	#production_methods
	investement_pool_borrowing = yes
	central_bank_production_methods = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_subject_custom_trigger = yes
		}
		central_bank_production_methods_2 = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_law = law_type:law_gold_exchange_standard
		}
		central_bank_production_methods_3 = yes
	}
}

	if = {
		not = {

		}
		gold_loaned_to_central_bank_fix = yes #attention ordre avec ai_buy_central_bank_debt
		 
	}
}

ai_building_strategy = {
	# limit = {
	# 	XXXXXXXXX
	# }

	#A chaque boucle 
	# - construction au niveau du pays 
	# - verifit si l'infrastructure est correct et l'ajoute
	# - Financial center maintenue au niveau maximum à voir 5 niveau max par boucle 

	# matière premiere dans tout les etat possible minimum 3 
	# 
	# - en fct des strategie du pays developpement de secteur 




	#idée coode
		#num_queued_private_constructions
	# construction_queue_num_queued_private_levels
	#construction_queue_private_duration





	#building_ef_private_construction
	if  = { #construit la difference de bd 
		limit  = {
			building_ef_private_construction_lvl_to_build > 0
		}

		#initialisation
		# while = {
		# 	count = building_ef_private_construction_lvl_to_build
		# 	random_scope_state = {
		# 		start_privately_funded_building_construction = building_ef_private_construction
		# 	}
		# }

		# random_scope_state = {
		# 	save_scope_as = state_target
		# }
		# scope:state_target = {

		#brut
		switch = {
			trigger = building_ef_private_construction_lvl_to_build
			1 = {
				random_scope_state = {
					limit ={
						or ={							
							not = {
								has_building = building_ef_private_construction
							}
							gdp > owner.gdp_05
							#gdp > owner.gdp_03
							#gdp > owner.gdp_04
						} 
					} 
					create_building = {
						building = building_ef_private_construction
						level = 1
					}
				}
			}
			2 = {
				random_scope_state = {
					limit ={
						or ={
							any_scope_building = {
								is_building_type = building_ef_private_construction
								level < 2
							}
							gdp > owner.gdp_05
							#gdp > owner.gdp_03
							#gdp > owner.gdp_04
						} 
					} 
					create_building = {
						building = building_ef_private_construction
						level = 2
					}
				}
			}
			3 = {
				random_scope_state = {
					limit ={
						or ={
							any_scope_building = {
								is_building_type = building_ef_private_construction
								level < 3
							}
							gdp > owner.gdp_05
							#gdp > owner.gdp_03
							#gdp > owner.gdp_04
						} 
					} 
					create_building = {
						building = building_ef_private_construction
						level = 3
					}
				}
			}
			4 = {
				random_scope_state = {
					limit ={
						or ={
							any_scope_building = {
								is_building_type = building_ef_private_construction
								level < 4
							}
							gdp > owner.gdp_05
							#gdp > owner.gdp_03
							#gdp > owner.gdp_04
						} 
					} 
					create_building = {
						building = building_ef_private_construction
						level = 4
					}
				}
			}
			5 = {
				random_scope_state = {
					limit ={
						or ={
							any_scope_building = {
								is_building_type = building_ef_private_construction
								level < 5
							}
							gdp > owner.gdp_05
							#gdp > owner.gdp_03
							#gdp > owner.gdp_04
						} 
					} 
					create_building = {
						building = building_ef_private_construction
						level = 5

				}
			}
			6 = {
				random_scope_state = {
					limit ={
						or ={
							any_scope_building = {

all_currency_resold = {
	#dinar
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			scope:target_country = {
				has_law = law_type:law_dinar_currency
				or = {
						var:currency_crisis = 1
					var:central_bank_bankruptcy = 1
				}
			}
			stockpiling_dinar_state > 0
		}
		sell_dinar_currency_crisis = yes
	}

RMSA_MMSA_order_trigger = {
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			or = {
				var:buy_grain_in_gold_1 = 1
				var:buy_grain_1 = 1
			}
		}
		buy_grain_order = yes
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			or = {
				var:sell_grain_in_gold_1 = 1
				var:sell_grain_1 = 1
			}
		}
		sell_grain_order = yes
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			or = {
				var:buy_wood_in_gold_1 = 1
				var:buy_wood_1 = 1
			}
		}
		buy_wood_order = yes
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			or = {
				var:sell_wood_in_gold_1 = 1
				var:sell_wood_1 = 1
			}
		}
		sell_wood_order = yes
	}
	if  = {
		limit  = {
			or = {
				var:buy_coal_in_gold_1 = 1
				var:buy_coal_1 = 1
			}
		}
		buy_coal_order = yes

	if  = {
		limit  = {
			or = {

update_modifiers_bc_fc_ns = {
	#si il n'a pas le batiment il ne délanche pas
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = {
				has_building = building_bank
			}
		}
		central_bank_modifier = yes
		regulation_law_gold_standard = yes

		stockpiling_capital_state_transfert = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = {
				or = {
					has_building = building_financial_centre
					has_building = building_financial_centre_fra
					has_building = building_financial_centre_gbr
					has_building = building_financial_centre_usa
					has_building = building_financial_centre_net
					has_building = building_financial_centre_ger
					has_building = building_financial_centre_aus
					has_building = building_financial_centre_ita
					has_building = building_financial_centre_chi
					has_building = building_financial_centre_jap
				}
			}
		}
		financial_center_modifier = yes

		stockpiling_capital_state_transfert = yes
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			any_scope_state = {
				has_building = building_national_stockpile
			}
		}
		national_stockpile_modifier = yes

		stockpiling_capital_state_transfert = yes
	}

	#si il n'a pas ou si il a. il déclanche
	#remove_state_building_modifier = yes
	remove_country_building_modifier = yes
	destroy_building_not_allowed = yes

	if  = {  #réinitialis la loi si un pays si lib
		limit = {
			law_currency_enacted = yes
			not  = {
				country_already_central_bank = yes
			}
		}
		remove_law_currency = yes
		regulation_law_gold_standard = yes
	}

	#test 
	#stockpiling_capital_state_transfert = yes
}
